<a id="954" class="Comment">-- Section 15.1 Commuting cubes</a>

<a id="987" class="Comment">-- Cubes</a>

  <a id="999" class="Comment">{- 
    We specify the type of the homotopy witnessing that a cube commutes. 
    Imagine that the cube is presented as a lattice
  
            *
          / | \
         /  |  \
        /   |   \
       *    *    *
       |\ /   \ /| 
       | \     ‌/ |
       |/ \   / \|
       *    *    *
        \   |   /
         \  |  /
          \ | /
            *

    with all maps pointing in the downwards direction. Presented in this way, a
    cube of maps has a top face, a back-left face, a back-right face, a 
    front-left face, a front-right face, and a bottom face, all of which are 
    homotopies.
  
    A term of type coherence-cube is a homotopy filling the cube.
  -}</a>

<a id="coherence-cube"></a><a id="1682" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#1682" class="Function">coherence-cube</a> <a id="1697" class="Symbol">:</a>
  <a id="1701" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="1702" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#1702" class="Bound">l1</a> <a id="1705" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#1705" class="Bound">l2</a> <a id="1708" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#1708" class="Bound">l3</a> <a id="1711" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#1711" class="Bound">l4</a> <a id="1714" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#1714" class="Bound">l1&#39;</a> <a id="1718" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#1718" class="Bound">l2&#39;</a> <a id="1722" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#1722" class="Bound">l3&#39;</a> <a id="1726" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#1726" class="Bound">l4&#39;</a> <a id="1730" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="1732" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="1737" class="Symbol">}</a>

<a id="2241" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#1682" class="Function">coherence-cube</a>

  <a id="4829" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4830" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4830" class="Bound">front-left</a> <a id="4841" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4843" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4844" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4519" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="4846" href="foundation-core.functions.html#420" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="4848" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4679" class="Bound">hB</a><a id="4850" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4852" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#627" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="4854" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4855" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4707" class="Bound">hD</a> <a id="4858" href="foundation-core.functions.html#420" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="4860" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4633" class="Bound">h&#39;</a><a id="4862" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="4906" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4907" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4907" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="4914" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4916" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4917" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4519" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="4919" href="foundation-core.functions.html#420" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="4921" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4495" class="Bound">f</a><a id="4922" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="4924" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#627" class="Function Operator">~</a> <a id="4926" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4927" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4531" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="4929" href="foundation-core.functions.html#420" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="4931" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4507" class="Bound">g</a><a id="4932" class="Symbol">))</a>
  <a id="4937" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="4938" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4938" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="4940" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="4942" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#1682" class="Function">coherence-cube</a>
    <a id="4961" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4495" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="4963" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4507" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="4965" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4519" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="4967" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4531" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="4969" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4603" class="Bound">f&#39;</a> <a id="4972" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4618" class="Bound">g&#39;</a> <a id="4975" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4633" class="Bound">h&#39;</a> <a id="4978" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4648" class="Bound">k&#39;</a> <a id="4981" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4665" class="Bound">hA</a> <a id="4984" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4679" class="Bound">hB</a> <a id="4987" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4693" class="Bound">hC</a> <a id="4990" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4707" class="Bound">hD</a>
    <a id="4997" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4723" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="5001" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4755" class="Bound">back-left</a> <a id="5011" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4792" class="Bound">back-right</a> <a id="5022" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4830" class="Bound">front-left</a> <a id="5033" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4868" class="Bound">front-right</a> <a id="5045" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4907" class="Bound">bottom</a><a id="5051" class="Symbol">)</a>
  <a id="5055" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="5064" class="Comment">{-
    The symmetry group D_3 acts on a cube. However, the coherence filling a
    a cube needs to be modified to show that the rotated/reflected cube again
    commutes. In the following definitions we provide the homotopies witnessing
    that the rotated/reflected cubes again commute.
  
    Note: although in principle it ought to be enough to show this for the
    generators of the symmetry group D_3, in practice it is more 
    straightforward to just do the work for each of the symmetries separately. 
    One reason is that some of the homotopies witnessing that the faces 
    commute will be inverted as the result of an application of a symmetry. 
    Inverting a homotopy twice results in a new homotopy that is only 
    homotopic to the original homotopy.

    We first provide some constructions involving homotopies that will help us
    manipulating coherences of cubes.
  -}</a>

  <a id="5964" class="Comment">-- We show that a rotation of a commuting cube again commutes.</a>
  <a id="Cubes.coherence-cube-rotate-120"></a><a id="6029" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#6029" class="Function">coherence-cube-rotate-120</a> <a id="6055" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="6061" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#1682" class="Function">coherence-cube</a>
      <a id="6082" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4693" class="Bound">hC</a> <a id="6085" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4648" class="Bound">k&#39;</a> <a id="6088" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4531" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="6090" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4707" class="Bound">hD</a> <a id="6093" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4665" class="Bound">hA</a> <a id="6096" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4603" class="Bound">f&#39;</a> <a id="6099" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4495" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="6101" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4679" class="Bound">hB</a> <a id="6104" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4618" class="Bound">g&#39;</a> <a id="6107" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4507" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="6109" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4633" class="Bound">h&#39;</a> <a id="6112" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4519" class="Bound">h</a>
      <a id="6120" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4755" class="Bound">back-left</a>
      <a id="6136" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6137" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#998" class="Function">inv-htpy</a> <a id="6146" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4792" class="Bound">back-right</a><a id="6156" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6158" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6159" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#998" class="Function">inv-htpy</a> <a id="6168" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4723" class="Bound">top</a><a id="6171" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="6179" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6180" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#998" class="Function">inv-htpy</a> <a id="6189" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4907" class="Bound">bottom</a><a id="6195" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6197" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6198" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#998" class="Function">inv-htpy</a> <a id="6207" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4830" class="Bound">front-left</a><a id="6217" class="Symbol">)</a>
      <a id="6225" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4868" class="Bound">front-right</a>
  <a id="6239" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#6029" class="Function">coherence-cube-rotate-120</a> <a id="6265" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#6265" class="Bound">a&#39;</a> <a id="6268" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="6274" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6276" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="6279" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="6282" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#6282" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="6284" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="6286" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#6282" class="Bound">t</a> <a id="6288" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#2425" class="Function Operator">∙</a> <a id="6290" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6291" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a> <a id="6294" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4519" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="6296" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6297" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#4755" class="Bound">back-left</a> <a id="6307" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#6265" class="Bound">a&#39;</a><a id="6309" class="Symbol">)))</a>

  <a id="7428" class="Comment">{- 
    We show that a reflection through the plane spanned by the vertices
    A&#39;, A, and D of a commuting cube again commutes.
  
    Note: Since the vertices A&#39; and D must always be fixed, the vertex A
    determines the mirror symmetry.
  -}</a>

  <a id="14100" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="14102" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#14089" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="14109" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2083" class="Function Operator">·r</a> <a id="14112" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#14027" class="Bound">hA</a><a id="14114" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="14116" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#1167" class="Function Operator">∙h</a> <a id="14119" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="14120" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#14013" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="14122" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#1877" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="14125" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#14055" class="Bound">back-right</a><a id="14135" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="14138" class="Comment">{-
coherence-htpy-square-rectangle-top-fl-rectangle-br-bot-cube : 
  {l1 l2 l3 l4 l1&#39; l2&#39; l3&#39; l4&#39; : Level}
  {A : UU l1} {B : UU l2} {C : UU l3} {D : UU l4}
  (f : A → B) (g : A → C) (h : B → D) (k : C → D)
  {A&#39; : UU l1&#39;} {B&#39; : UU l2&#39;} {C&#39; : UU l3&#39;} {D&#39; : UU l4&#39;}
  (f&#39; : A&#39; → B&#39;) (g&#39; : A&#39; → C&#39;) (h&#39; : B&#39; → D&#39;) (k&#39; : C&#39; → D&#39;)
  (hA : A&#39; → A) (hB : B&#39; → B) (hC : C&#39; → C) (hD : D&#39; → D)
  (top : (h&#39; ∘ f&#39;) ~ (k&#39; ∘ g&#39;))
  (back-left : (f ∘ hA) ~ (hB ∘ f&#39;))
  (back-right : (g ∘ hA) ~ (hC ∘ g&#39;))
  (front-left : (h ∘ hB) ~ (hD ∘ h&#39;))
  (front-right : (k ∘ hC) ~ (hD ∘ k&#39;))
  (bottom : (h ∘ f) ~ (k ∘ g))
  (c : coherence-cube f g h k f&#39; g&#39; h&#39; k&#39; hA hB hC hD
    top back-left back-right front-left front-right bottom) →
  coherence-htpy-square
    ( inv-htpy front-right)
    ( refl-htpy&#39; h)
    ( pair g&#39; (pair (hB ∘ f&#39;)
      ( inv-htpy (rectangle-top-front-left-cube f g h k f&#39; g&#39; h&#39; k&#39; hA hB hC hD
        top back-left back-right front-left front-right bottom))))
    ( pair g&#39; (pair (f ∘ hA)
      ( inv-htpy
        ( rectangle-back-right-bottom-cube f g h k f&#39; g&#39; h&#39; k&#39; hA hB hC hD
          top back-left back-right front-left front-right bottom))))
    ( refl-htpy&#39; g&#39;)
    ( inv-htpy back-left)
coherence-htpy-square-rectangle-top-fl-rectangle-br-bot-cube = {!!}
-}</a>

<a id="16017" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#15412" class="Function">rectangle-top-front-right-cube</a>
  <a id="16050" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16050" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="16052" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16052" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="16054" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16054" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="16056" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16056" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="16058" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16058" class="Bound">f&#39;</a> <a id="16061" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16061" class="Bound">g&#39;</a> <a id="16064" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16064" class="Bound">h&#39;</a> <a id="16067" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16067" class="Bound">k&#39;</a> <a id="16070" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16070" class="Bound">hA</a> <a id="16073" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16073" class="Bound">hB</a> <a id="16076" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16076" class="Bound">hC</a> <a id="16079" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16079" class="Bound">hD</a>
  <a id="16084" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16084" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="16088" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16088" class="Bound">back-left</a> <a id="16098" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16098" class="Bound">back-right</a> <a id="16109" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16109" class="Bound">front-left</a> <a id="16120" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16120" class="Bound">front-right</a> <a id="16132" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16132" class="Bound">bottom</a> <a id="16139" class="Symbol">=</a>
  <a id="16143" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16144" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16079" class="Bound">hD</a> <a id="16147" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#1877" class="Function Operator">·l</a> <a id="16150" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16084" class="Bound">top</a><a id="16153" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16155" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#1167" class="Function Operator">∙h</a> <a id="16158" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16159" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#998" class="Function">inv-htpy</a> <a id="16168" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="16169" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16120" class="Bound">front-right</a><a id="16180" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="16182" href="foundation-core.homotopies.html#2083" class="Function Operator">·r</a> <a id="16185" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16061" class="Bound">g&#39;</a><a id="16187" class="Symbol">)</a>

<a id="rectangle-back-left-bottom-cube"></a><a id="16190" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16190" class="Function">rectangle-back-left-bottom-cube</a> <a id="16222" class="Symbol">:</a>

<a id="16793" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16190" class="Function">rectangle-back-left-bottom-cube</a>
  <a id="16827" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16827" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="16829" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16829" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="16831" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16831" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="16833" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16833" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="16835" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16835" class="Bound">f&#39;</a> <a id="16838" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16838" class="Bound">g&#39;</a> <a id="16841" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16841" class="Bound">h&#39;</a> <a id="16844" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16844" class="Bound">k&#39;</a> <a id="16847" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16847" class="Bound">hA</a> <a id="16850" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16850" class="Bound">hB</a> <a id="16853" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16853" class="Bound">hC</a> <a id="16856" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#16856" class="Bound">hD</a>

  <a id="25433" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="25434" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25434" class="Bound">c</a> <a id="25436" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="25438" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#1682" class="Function">coherence-cube</a> <a id="25453" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#24989" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="25455" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25001" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="25457" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25013" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="25459" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25025" class="Bound">k</a> <a id="25461" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25097" class="Bound">f&#39;</a> <a id="25464" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25112" class="Bound">g&#39;</a> <a id="25467" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25127" class="Bound">h&#39;</a> <a id="25470" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25142" class="Bound">k&#39;</a> <a id="25473" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25159" class="Bound">hA</a> <a id="25476" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25173" class="Bound">hB</a> <a id="25479" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25187" class="Bound">hC</a> <a id="25482" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25201" class="Bound">hD</a>
       <a id="25492" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25217" class="Bound">top</a> <a id="25496" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25249" class="Bound">back-left</a> <a id="25506" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25286" class="Bound">back-right</a> <a id="25517" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25324" class="Bound">front-left</a> <a id="25528" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25362" class="Bound">front-right</a> <a id="25540" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#25401" class="Bound">bottom</a><a id="25546" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="25548" class="Symbol">→</a>

<a id="32486" class="Comment">-- Section 15.2 Fiberwise pullbacks.</a>

<a id="32524" class="Comment">{- We show that if we have a square of families, such that the base square is
   a pullback square, then each square of fibers is a pullback square if and
   only if the square of total spaces is a pullback square. -}</a>

        <a id="44522" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="44524" href="foundation-core.contractible-types.html#4047" class="Function">is-equiv-is-contr</a> <a id="44542" class="Symbol">_</a>

          <a id="44590" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="44592" href="foundation-core.contractible-types.html#2046" class="Function">is-contr-total-path</a> <a id="44612" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="44613" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#43494" class="Bound">p</a> <a id="44615" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#43516" class="Bound">c1</a><a id="44617" class="Symbol">))))</a>
      <a id="44628" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="44630" href="synthetic-homotopy-theory.25-cubical-diagrams.html#43519" class="Bound">c2</a><a id="44632" class="Symbol">))</a>

<a id="44636" class="Comment">{- Next we show that for any commuting cube, if the bottom and top squares are
   pullback squares, then so is the square of fibers of the vertical maps in
   cube. -}</a>

<a id="44805" class="Comment">{-

square-fib-cube :
  {l1 l2 l3 l4 l1&#39; l2&#39; l3&#39; l4&#39; : Level}
  {A : UU l1} {B : UU l2} {C : UU l3} {D : UU l4}
  (f : A → B) (g : A → C) (h : B → D) (k : C → D)
  {A&#39; : UU l1&#39;} {B&#39; : UU l2&#39;} {C&#39; : UU l3&#39;} {D&#39; : UU l4&#39;}
  (f&#39; : A&#39; → B&#39;) (g&#39; : A&#39; → C&#39;) (h&#39; : B&#39; → D&#39;) (k&#39; : C&#39; → D&#39;)
  (hA : A&#39; → A) (hB : B&#39; → B) (hC : C&#39; → C) (hD : D&#39; → D)
  (top : (h&#39; ∘ f&#39;) ~ (k&#39; ∘ g&#39;))
  (back-left : (f ∘ hA) ~ (hB ∘ f&#39;))
  (back-right : (g ∘ hA) ~ (hC ∘ g&#39;))
  (front-left : (h ∘ hB) ~ (hD ∘ h&#39;))
  (front-right : (k ∘ hC) ~ (hD ∘ k&#39;))
  (bottom : (h ∘ f) ~ (k ∘ g)) →
  (c : coherence-cube f g h k f&#39; g&#39; h&#39; k&#39; hA hB hC hD
       top back-left back-right front-left front-right bottom) →
  (a : A) →
  ( ( tot (λ d&#39; p → p ∙ (bottom a)) ∘
      ( map-fib-cone h hD (pair hB (pair h&#39; front-left)) (f a))) ∘
    ( map-fib-cone f hB (pair hA (pair f&#39; back-left)) a)) ~
  ( ( map-fib-cone k hD (pair hC (pair k&#39; front-right)) (g a)) ∘
    ( map-fib-cone g hC (pair hA (pair g&#39; back-right)) a))
square-fib-cube f g h k f&#39; g&#39; h&#39; k&#39; hA hB hC hD
  top back-left back-right front-left front-right bottom c
  .(hA a&#39;) (pair a&#39; refl) =
  eq-pair-Σ
    ( pair
      ( top a&#39;)
      ( ( tr-id-left-subst
          ( top a&#39;)
          ( k (g (hA a&#39;)))
          ( ( ( inv (front-left (f&#39; a&#39;))) ∙
              ( ap h ((inv (back-left a&#39;)) ∙ refl))) ∙
            ( bottom (hA a&#39;)))) ∙
        ( ( ( assoc (inv (ap hD (top a&#39;))) _ (bottom (hA a&#39;))) ∙
            {!!}) ∙
          ( distributive-inv-concat (ap k (back-right a&#39;)) (front-right (g&#39; a&#39;)) ∙
            ( ( ap
                ( concat (inv (front-right (g&#39; a&#39;))) ?)
                ( inv (ap-inv k (back-right a&#39;)))) ∙
              ( ap
                ( concat (inv (front-right (g&#39; a&#39;))) ?)
                ( ap (ap k) (inv right-unit))))))))
-}</a>
</pre>
